data-hovercard="/ajax/hovercard/user.php?id=100004999891350&amp;extragetparams=%7B%22hc_location%22%3A%22stream%22%7D">LeideeCorp Gaming</a></div></h5><h5 class="uiStreamMessage recentStoryText" data-ft="&#123;&quot;type&quot;:1,&quot;tn&quot;:&quot;K&quot;&#125;"> <span class="messageBody" data-ft="&#123;&quot;type&quot;:3&#125;">LeideeCorp

Introduction

LeideeCorp is requesting bids for three logo designs. Our company will award this contract on a competitive basis.

Instructions for Completing the Proposal

The proposal needs to be as brief and accurate as possible. Submit three samples of previous logo designs you have done.

Proposal Deadline

All proposals must be emailed no later than 5:00 PM, Friday, April 26, 2013. Submit your proposal to LeideeCorp at the following email:

		ivandeleon&#064;leideecorp.com

Project Evaluation 

Each submittal will be evaluated on a competitive basis against other proposals submitted by other interested applicants.  

Meetings between the vendor and LeideeCorp to review the proposals will be scheduled and confirmed by April 29, 2013.

PROJECT DESCRIPTION

1.	Project Liaison. Designate a contact person who will serve as the liaison between LeideeCorp and your organization for all matters pertaining to this proposal.  Include the person’s name, title, email address, and telephone.

2.	Proposal.  Needs to contain the following:

a.	Total Cost – Identify the total cost for three different logo designs based on the following specifications:
i.	Logo color – orange, blue and purple
ii.	Size –  300 mega pixels
iii.	Format – master
b.	Estimated time it will take you to complete three logo designs.
c.	Submit three samples of previous logo designs you have done.

3.	Project due Date.	  Proposal is due by 5:00 PM, April 26, 2013.
4.	Start Date.   Following vendor selection, project will start immediately.

Internships available in all areas.

For more information please contact:
